It is meant to be simple and with as few confusing elements as possible.\r\n\r\nPeriod:\r\nWhen you have entered your first period, the system will calculate and show you when you can expect to get your next period, or any period in the future.\r\nP-pills:\r\nBesides helping you to remember/see when you should expect to have your next period (and not least when you are not having your period), the system can help you remember to take your p-pill (if enabled).\r\nThe system visualizes when you are supposed to take the pill and if you have already taken it.\r\n\r\nReminder before your period:\r\nThe system can remind you of your next period. You can set how many days before and at which time of the day you want the reminder.\r\n \r\nP-pill reminder:\r\nThe system can remind you to take your p-pill every day in the period where you are supposed to take it. You can decide at which time of the day to get the reminder.\r\n\r\nNotes and symbols:\r\nYou can write notes on any day, and set symbols indicating pain, illness, extra bleeding etc.\r\nThat way you can keep a diary for your period, or practically anything regarding your period/p-pills.\r\nLive Tiles:\r\nPeriod Control supports live tiles to keep you informed.
